python35 in fedora-32

This page displays detail informations of the python35 package. You might want go back to the main page of python35.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-02-19 Petr Viktorin - 3.5.10-5 - Fix FTBFS on ppc64le and x86-64 Resolves: https://bugzilla.redhat.com/show_bug.cgi?id=1923654 Resolves: https://bugzilla.redhat.com/show_bug.cgi?id=1923658

2020-08-06 Lumír Balhar - 3.5.9-8 - Add support for upstream architectures' names (patch 353)
